Now I see the key difference. For normal upstream responses in `onUpstreamHeaders` at lines 1792-1793:```cpp\nroute_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders(*headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());\nmodify_headers_(*headers);\n```\n\nThis is called ONCE, and then `callbacks_->encodeHeaders` is called at line 1799.\n\nBut for local replies in `onUpstreamAbort` at lines 1403-1412:```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(    code, body,    [dropped, this](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers) {      if (dropped && !config_->suppress_envoy_headers_) {\n        headers.addReference(Http::Headers::get().EnvoyOverloaded,                             Http::Headers::get().EnvoyOverloadedValues.True);\n      }\n      modify_headers_(headers);  // <-- calls modify_headers_    },\n    absl::nullopt, details);```\n\nAnd then in the filter manager's `prepareLocalReply` or `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain` (lines 1072-1079 or 1123-1130), it creates ANOTHER callback that ALSO calls `finalizeResponseHeaders`:\n\n```cpp\n[this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {  if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {    streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, streamInfo());  }  if (modify_headers) {    modify_headers(headers);  }},```\n\nSo the issue is:\n1. Router calls `sendLocalReply` with a lambda that calls `modify_headers_`\n2. The filter manager ALSO calls `finalizeResponseHeaders` in its own callback\n3. When the filter manager calls the `modify_headers` callback passed from the router, it calls `modify_headers_`, which is just the attempted count thing, not finalizeResponseHeaders\n\n\n4. The user mentions that the headers are duplicated in \"local replies but not on proxied upstream responses\". {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_0191g7D16ijieuBoaCNCcCZQ","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I have a clear picture. The issue is that the router's `modify_headers_` is initialized during `decodeHeaders` and only adds attempt count. It doesn't call `finalizeResponseHeaders`.\n\nBut the filter manager's callback for local replies DOES call `finalizeResponseHeaders` and then calls the `modify_headers` lambda (which is the router's lambda).\n\nSo there should be only ONE call to `finalizeResponseHeaders` for local replies.\n\nBUT... what if the issue is that the callback is being invoked TWICE? Or what if the problem is that the filter manager's callback is being invoked in ADDITION to something else also calling `finalizeResponseHeaders`?\n\nActually, let me reconsider the whole scenario. The user says the headers are duplicated for LOCAL REPLIES but not for PROXIED responses. This suggests that there's something different about how local replies are handled vs. proxied responses.\n\nFor proxied responses (upstream):\n1. Router calls `finalizeResponseHeaders` at line 1792\n2. Router calls `modify_headers_` at line 1793\n3. Router calls `callbacks_->encodeHeaders(...)` at line 1799\n\nFor local replies:\n1. Router calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply(code, body, [modify_headers lambda], ...)`\n2. Filter manager calls `prepareLocalReply` which invokes the callback:   a. `finalizeResponseHeaders`   b. `modify_headers` lambda which calls `modify_headers_`\n3. Then `executeLocalReplyIfPrepared` is called which invokes `encodeLocalReply`\n\nSo both cases should only call `finalizeResponseHeaders` once. But wait... what if there's a case where BOTH the router's lambda AND the filter manager's callback are calling `finalizeResponseHeaders`?\n\nLet me check the direct response case again. In lines 486-503:\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(    direct_response->responseCode(), direct_response->responseBody(),    [this, direct_response, &request_headers = headers](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {      ...      direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(response_headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());    },    ...);\n\n\n```\n\nSo the router's lambda DOES call `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders`! And then the filter manager's callback ALSO calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders`! So there are TWO calls! This could be the source of the duplication for direct responses. For other local replies like upstream timeouts, the router's lambda doesn't call `finalizeResponseHeaders`, so there's only one call. The user mentioned upstream timeout specifically, so I need to check if that scenario also has this double-call issue or if it's something else entirely.\n\nLooking at the timeout path through `onUpstreamAbort`, it doesn't invoke `finalizeResponseHeaders` from the router's lambda. So where would the duplication occur there? Maybe the filter manager is invoking the `modify_headers` callback multiple times, or perhaps `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain` gets called twice in some code path. When `sendLocalReply` is triggered, it invokes either `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain` or `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain`, both of which set up callbacks containing `finalizeResponseHeaders`. The question is whether these callbacks are being executed more than once or if there's another code path causing the headers to be finalized twice.\n```\n\ncpp\nroute_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders(*headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());\nmodify_headers_(*headers);\n```\n\nFor upstream responses, `finalizeResponseHeaders` runs once before `encodeHeaders` at line 1799. But with local replies, the flow differs: the router calls `sendLocalReply` with a lambda, then the filter manager invokes `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain` or similar, which should also call The issue stems from `finalizeResponseHeaders()` being called by both the router's lambda callback AND the filter manager's header modification callback, causing response headers to be added twice despite `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` semantics.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe duplication occurs due to a mismatch in responsibility between how the router handles upstream responses vs. local replies:\n\n1. **For upstream responses** (`onUpstreamHeaders`): Router calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` directly at line 1792, then `modify_headers_` at line 1793, then `encodeHeaders()` at line 1799\n2. **For local replies** (`onUpstreamAbort`, direct responses): Router calls `sendLocalReply()` with a lambda that calls `modify_headers_`, and the filter manager INDEPENDENTLY calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its header modification callback\n\nThis creates a scenario where:\n- **Direct responses**: The router's lambda invokes `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (line 501 in router.cc)\n- **Filter manager callback**: The filter manager's callback invokes `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (line 1074 in filter_manager.cc)\n- Result: Headers are added twice if both the direct response entry and the route entry have the same headers configured\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Code References\n\n**Router filter - sendLocalReply for upstream abort (router.cc:1403-1412)**:\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    code, body,\n    [dropped, this](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers) {\n      if (dropped && !config_->suppress_envoy_headers_) {\n        headers.addReference(...);\n      }\n      modify_headers_(headers);  // <-- Calls modify_headers_, not finalizeResponseHeaders\n    },\n    ...);\n```\n\n**Router filter - sendLocalReply for direct responses (router.cc:486-503)**:\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    direct_response->responseCode(),\n    direct_response->responseBody(),\n    [this, direct_response, ...](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {\n      ...\n      direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(response_headers, ...);  // <-- FIRST CALL\n    },\n    ...);\n```\n\n**Filter manager - prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain (filter_manager.cc:1072-1078)**:\n```cpp\n[this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {\n  if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n    streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, ...);  // <-- SECOND CALL\n  }\n  if (modify_headers) {\n    modify_headers(headers);  // Invokes router's lambda\n  }\n},\n```\n\n**Filter manager - sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain (filter_manager.cc:1123-1130)**:\nSame pattern as prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain\n\n**Utility - prepareLocalReply invocation (utility.cc:718-720)**:\n```cpp\nif (encode_functions.modify_headers_) {\n  encode_functions.modify_headers_(*response_headers);  // <-- Invokes filter manager's callback\n}\n```\n\n### Call Chain for Direct Responses\n\n1. Router's `onResponseDirect()` calls `sendLocalReply()` with lambda containing `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n2. Filter manager's `sendLocalReply()` → `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n3. `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` calls `Utility::sendLocalReply()`\n4. `Utility::sendLocalReply()` calls `prepareLocalReply()`\n5. `prepareLocalReply()` invokes `encode_functions.modify_headers_()` callback from filter manager\n6. Filter manager's callback calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (already called by router's lambda!)\n7. Result: **Headers added twice**\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **source/common/router/router.cc**:\n   - `Filter::onResponseDirect()` - passes direct response lambda to `sendLocalReply`\n   - `Filter::onUpstreamAbort()` - passes abort handler lambda to `sendLocalReply`\n   - `Filter::decodeHeaders()` - initializes `modify_headers_` member\n\n2. **source/common/http/filter_manager.cc**:\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` - dispatches to `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` or `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` - creates callback with `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` - creates callback with `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendDirectLocalReply()` - creates callback with `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n\n3. **source/common/http/utility.cc**:\n   - `Utility::prepareLocalReply()` - invokes the modify_headers callback\n   - `Utility::sendLocalReply()` - orchestrates local reply preparation and encoding\n\n4. **source/common/router/config_impl.cc**:\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::finalizeResponseHeaders()` - applies response header parsers\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::getResponseHeaderParsers()` - retrieves parsers for finalization\n\n5. **api/envoy/config/core/v3/base.proto**:\n   - `HeaderValueOption.append_action` enum - controls header append behavior\n   - Deprecated `append` BoolValue field - legacy append control\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom**: Duplicate response headers in access logs for local replies (e.g., two `x-custom-trace` headers)\n2. **Router behavior**: For direct responses, router's lambda calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n3. **Filter manager intercept**: Filter manager's `sendLocalReply()` creates its own callback\n4. **Callback creation**: Filter manager's callback includes BOTH `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` AND router's lambda\n5. **Header evaluation**: `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()`\n6. **Header parser logic**: Parser uses `setReferenceKey()` for `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`, but since called twice, both instances add headers\n7. **Root cause**: `finalizeResponseHeaders()` invoked twice in sequence:\n   - First by router's lambda (for direct responses)\n   - Second by filter manager's callback\n8. **Symptom manifestation**: Headers appear twice in response because `evaluateHeaders()` was called twice on the same header map\n\n## Recommendation\n\n**Fix Strategy**: The filter manager should NOT call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its local reply callback if the router's lambda has already invoked it.\n\n**Implementation Options**:\n\n1. **Option A** (Recommended): Router should NOT invoke `finalizeResponseHeaders()` from the lambda passed to `sendLocalReply()`. Instead, rely solely on the filter manager to call it once. Modify:\n   - `Filter::onResponseDirect()` - remove `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call from lambda\n   - Let filter manager's callback handle all response header finalization\n\n2. **Option B**: Filter manager should track if `finalizeResponseHeaders()` has already been called in the router's lambda and skip its own invocation. This requires explicit coordination between router and filter manager.\n\n3. **Option C**: Create a separate code path for direct responses that doesn't use the filter manager's header modification callback for `finalizeResponseHeaders()`.\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. Check if headers are duplicated specifically for direct responses (redirect routes) vs. timeout-generated local replies\n2. Verify the `append_action` proto field values in the route configuration\n3. Trace `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()` calls using debug logging at lines 947 and 1074\n4. The issue stems from `finalizeResponseHeaders()` being called by both the router's lambda callback AND the filter manager's header modification callback, causing response headers to be added twice despite `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` semantics.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe duplication occurs due to a mismatch in responsibility between how the router handles upstream responses vs. local replies:\n\n1. **For upstream responses** (`onUpstreamHeaders`): Router calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` directly at line 1792, then `modify_headers_` at line 1793, then `encodeHeaders()` at line 1799\n2. **For local replies** (`onUpstreamAbort`, direct responses): Router calls `sendLocalReply()` with a lambda that calls `modify_headers_`, and the filter manager INDEPENDENTLY calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its header modification callback\n\nThis creates a scenario where:\n- **Direct responses**: The router's lambda invokes `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (line 501 in router.cc)\n- **Filter manager callback**: The filter manager's callback invokes `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (line 1074 in filter_manager.cc)\n- Result: Headers are added twice if both the direct response entry and the route entry have the same headers configured\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Code References\n\n**Router filter - sendLocalReply for upstream abort (router.cc:1403-1412)**:\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    code, body,\n    [dropped, this](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers) {\n      if (dropped && !config_->suppress_envoy_headers_) {\n        headers.addReference(...);\n      }\n      modify_headers_(headers);  // <-- Calls modify_headers_, not finalizeResponseHeaders\n    },\n    ...);\n```\n\n**Router filter - sendLocalReply for direct responses (router.cc:486-503)**:\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    direct_response->responseCode(),\n    direct_response->responseBody(),\n    [this, direct_response, ...](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {\n      ...\n      direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(response_headers, ...);  // <-- FIRST CALL\n    },\n    ...);\n```\n\n**Filter manager - prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain (filter_manager.cc:1072-1078)**:\n```cpp\n[this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {\n  if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n    streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, ...);  // <-- SECOND CALL\n  }\n  if (modify_headers) {\n    modify_headers(headers);  // Invokes router's lambda\n  }\n},\n```\n\n**Filter manager - sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain (filter_manager.cc:1123-1130)**:\nSame pattern as prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain\n\n**Utility - prepareLocalReply invocation (utility.cc:718-720)**:\n```cpp\nif (encode_functions.modify_headers_) {\n  encode_functions.modify_headers_(*response_headers);  // <-- Invokes filter manager's callback\n}\n```\n\n### Call Chain for Direct Responses\n\n1. Router's `onResponseDirect()` calls `sendLocalReply()` with lambda containing `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n2. Filter manager's `sendLocalReply()` → `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n3. `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` calls `Utility::sendLocalReply()`\n4. `Utility::sendLocalReply()` calls `prepareLocalReply()`\n5. `prepareLocalReply()` invokes `encode_functions.modify_headers_()` callback from filter manager\n6. Filter manager's callback calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (already called by router's lambda!)\n7. Result: **Headers added twice**\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **source/common/router/router.cc**:\n   - `Filter::onResponseDirect()` - passes direct response lambda to `sendLocalReply`\n   - `Filter::onUpstreamAbort()` - passes abort handler lambda to `sendLocalReply`\n   - `Filter::decodeHeaders()` - initializes `modify_headers_` member\n\n2. **source/common/http/filter_manager.cc**:\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` - dispatches to `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` or `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` - creates callback with `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` - creates callback with `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendDirectLocalReply()` - creates callback with `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n\n3. **source/common/http/utility.cc**:\n   - `Utility::prepareLocalReply()` - invokes the modify_headers callback\n   - `Utility::sendLocalReply()` - orchestrates local reply preparation and encoding\n\n4. **source/common/router/config_impl.cc**:\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::finalizeResponseHeaders()` - applies response header parsers\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::getResponseHeaderParsers()` - retrieves parsers for finalization\n\n5. **api/envoy/config/core/v3/base.proto**:\n   - `HeaderValueOption.append_action` enum - controls header append behavior\n   - Deprecated `append` BoolValue field - legacy append control\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom**: Duplicate response headers in access logs for local replies (e.g., two `x-custom-trace` headers)\n2. **Router behavior**: For direct responses, router's lambda calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n3. **Filter manager intercept**: Filter manager's `sendLocalReply()` creates its own callback\n4. **Callback creation**: Filter manager's callback includes BOTH `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` AND router's lambda\n5. **Header evaluation**: `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()`\n6. **Header parser logic**: Parser uses `setReferenceKey()` for `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`, but since called twice, both instances add headers\n7. **Root cause**: `finalizeResponseHeaders()` invoked twice in sequence:\n   - First by router's lambda (for direct responses)\n   - Second by filter manager's callback\n8. **Symptom manifestation**: Headers appear twice in response because `evaluateHeaders()` was called twice on the same header map\n\n## Recommendation\n\n**Fix Strategy**: The filter manager should NOT call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its local reply callback if the router's lambda has already invoked it.\n\n**Implementation Options**:\n\n1. **Option A** (Recommended): Router should NOT invoke `finalizeResponseHeaders()` from the lambda passed to `sendLocalReply()`. Instead, rely solely on the filter manager to call it once. Modify:\n   - `Filter::onResponseDirect()` - remove `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call from lambda\n   - Let filter manager's callback handle all response header finalization\n\n2. **Option B**: Filter manager should track if `finalizeResponseHeaders()` has already been called in the router's lambda and skip its own invocation. This requires explicit coordination between router and filter manager.\n\n3. **Option C**: Create a separate code path for direct responses that doesn't use the filter manager's header modification callback for `finalizeResponseHeaders()`.\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. Check if headers are duplicated specifically for direct responses (redirect routes) vs. timeout-generated local replies\n2. Verify the `append_action` proto field values in the route configuration\n3. Trace `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()` calls using debug logging at lines 947 and 1074\n4. Confirm if `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` and `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()` are both being invoked\n5. Check if similar duplication occurs with `request_headers_to_add` for early header mutations in the reverse direction\n\n## Proto Field Considerations\n\n**HeaderValueOption.append_action** (api/envoy/config/core/v3/base.proto:476):\n- `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`: Uses `addReferenceKey()` - always appends\n- `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`: Uses `setReferenceKey()` - replaces if exists, adds if absent\n- `ADD_IF_ABSENT`: Uses `addReferenceKey()` conditionally - only adds if missing\n- `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS`: Uses `setReferenceKey()` conditionally - only if exists\n\nLegacy **append** BoolValue field is deprecated in favor of `append_action` enum (source/common/router/header_parser.cc:58-63), but both may be present in configs requiring compatibility handling.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
